226	function Literal(lex, languageOrDatatype, _native) {
227	    this.lex = lex;
228	    var ndict;
229	    if (languageOrDatatype.isURI && languageOrDatatype.isURI()) {
230	        this.language = "";  // Language cannot be null, be empty string
231	        this.datatype = languageOrDatatype;
232	        ndict = {'0': lex, '1': languageOrDatatype, '2': null};
233	    } else {
234	        var _lang = ""+languageOrDatatype;
235	        this.language = _lang;
236	        this.datatype = new NamedNode("http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#langString");
237	        ndict = {'0': lex, '1': null, '2': languageOrDatatype};
238	    }
239	    if (! _native) {
240	        _native = _make_literal(ndict);
241	    }
242	    this._native = _native;
243	}
244	Literal.from_native = function(native) {
245	    var lex = native.lexical;
246	    var languageOrDatatype;
247	    var lang = native.language;
248	    var dt = native.datatype;
249	    if (lang) {
250	        languageOrDatatype = ""+lang;
251	    } else if (dt) {
252	        languageOrDatatype = new NamedNode(dt);
253	    } else {
254	        languageOrDatatype = new NamedNode("http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string");
255	    }
256	    return new Literal(lex, languageOrDatatype, native);
257	}
258	Literal.prototype.toPython = function() { return this._native; }
259	Literal.prototype.toString = function() { return "Literal("+this.lex+", dt="+this.datatype+", lang='"+this.language+"')"; }
260	Literal.prototype.isURI = function() { return false; }
261	Literal.prototype.isBlankNode = function() { return false; }
262	Literal.prototype.isLiteral = function() { return true; }
263	Literal.prototype.equals = function(other) {
264	    if (other.constructor && other.constructor === Literal) {
265	        return _native_node_equals({'0': this._native, '1': other._native});
266	    }
267	    return false;
268	}

>> Issue: [B824:url_found] url_found
   Severity: Medium   Confidence: Medium
   Location: /home/blue/PyPIAgent/Dataset/study/unzip_benign/pyshacl-0.30.1/pyshacl-0.30.1/test/issues/issue_102.py:4

4	qb_shacl = '''\
5	# baseURI: http://topbraid.org/datacube
6	# imports: http://datashapes.org/dash
7	# imports: http://purl.org/linked-data/cube
8	# imports: http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core
9	
10	@prefix dash: <http://datashapes.org/dash#> .
11	@prefix owl: <http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#> .
12	@prefix qb: <http://purl.org/linked-data/cube#> .
13	@prefix rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#> .
14	@prefix rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> .
15	@prefix sh: <http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#> .
16	@prefix skos: <http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#> .
17	@prefix xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> .
18	
19	<http://topbraid.org/datacube>
20	  rdf:type owl:Ontology ;
21	  rdfs:comment "Implements the integrity constraints defined by section 11.1 of the Data Cube specification. Most of the constraints work in standard SHACL-SPARQL, but two constraints require a SHACL function (from SHACL Advanced Features) to recursively walk a dynamically computed property path. An alternative implementation of these constraints could be produced without a helper function based on SHACL-JS." ;
22	  rdfs:label "SHACL shapes for RDF Data Cube Vocabulary" ;
23	  rdfs:seeAlso <https://www.w3.org/TR/vocab-data-cube/#wf-rules> ;
24	  owl:imports <http://datashapes.org/dash> ;
25	  owl:imports <http://purl.org/linked-data/cube> ;
26	  owl:imports <http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core> ;
27	  owl:versionInfo "Created with TopBraid Composer. This is currently completely untested." ;
28	  sh:declare [
29	      rdf:type sh:PrefixDeclaration ;
30	      sh:namespace "http://purl.org/linked-data/cube#"^^xsd:anyURI ;
31	      sh:prefix "qb" ;
32	    ] ;
33	.
34	
35	qb:ObservationShape
36	  rdf:type sh:NodeShape ;
37	  rdfs:label "Observation shape" ;
38	  sh:property [
39	      sh:path qb:dataSet ;
40	      rdfs:comment "IC-1. Unique DataSet" ;
41	      sh:maxCount 1 ;
42	      sh:message "Every qb:Observation has exactly one associated qb:DataSet." ;
43	      sh:minCount 1 ;
44	    ] ;
45	  sh:sparql [
46	      rdfs:comment "IC-11. All dimensions required" ;
47	      sh:message "Every qb:Observation has a value for each dimension declared in its associated qb:DataStructureDefinition." ;
48	      sh:prefixes <http://topbraid.org/datacube> ;
49	      sh:select """SELECT $this
50	WHERE {
51		$this qb:dataSet/qb:structure/qb:component/qb:componentProperty ?dim .
52	    ?dim a qb:DimensionProperty;
53	    FILTER NOT EXISTS { $this ?dim [] }
54	}""" ;
55	    ] ;
56	  sh:sparql [
57	      rdfs:comment "IC-12. No duplicate observations" ;
58	      sh:message "No two qb:Observations in the same qb:DataSet may have the same value for all dimensions." ;
59	      sh:prefixes <http://topbraid.org/datacube> ;
60	      sh:select """SELECT $this
61	WHERE {
62		{
63			# For each pair of observations test if all the dimension values are the same
64			SELECT $this (MIN(?equal) AS ?allEqual)
65			WHERE {
66				$this qb:dataSet ?dataset .
67				?obs2 qb:dataSet ?dataset .
68				FILTER ($this != ?obs2)
69				?dataset qb:structure/qb:component/qb:componentProperty ?dim .
70				?dim a qb:DimensionProperty .
71				$this ?dim ?value1 .
72				?obs2 ?dim ?value2 .
73				BIND( ?value1 = ?value2 AS ?equal)
74			}
75			GROUP BY $this ?obs2
76		}
77		FILTER( ?allEqual )
78	}""" ;
79	    ] ;
80	  sh:sparql [
81	      rdfs:comment "IC-13. Required attributes" ;
82	      sh:message "Every qb:Observation has a value for each declared attribute that is marked as required." ;
83	      sh:prefixes <http://topbraid.org/datacube> ;
84	      sh:select """SELECT $this
85	WHERE {
86		$this qb:dataSet/qb:structure/qb:component ?component .
87		?component qb:componentRequired true ;
88			qb:componentProperty ?attr .
89		FILTER NOT EXISTS { $this ?attr [] }
90	}""" ;
91	    ] ;
92	  sh:sparql [
93	      rdfs:comment "IC-14. All measures present" ;
94	      sh:message "In a qb:DataSet which does not use a Measure dimension then each individual qb:Observation must have a value for every declared measure." ;
95	      sh:prefixes <http://topbraid.org/datacube> ;
96	      sh:select """SELECT $this
97	WHERE {
98		# Observation in a non-measureType cube
99		$this qb:dataSet/qb:structure ?dsd .
100		FILTER NOT EXISTS { ?dsd qb:component/qb:componentProperty qb:measureType }
101		# verify every measure is present
102		?dsd qb:component/qb:componentProperty ?measure .
103		?measure a qb:MeasureProperty;
104		FILTER NOT EXISTS { $this ?measure [] }
105	}""" ;
106	    ] ;
107	  sh:sparql [
108	      rdfs:comment "IC-15. Measure dimension consistent" ;
109	      sh:message "In a qb:DataSet which uses a Measure dimension then each qb:Observation must have a value for the measure corresponding to its given qb:measureType." ;
110	      sh:prefixes <http://topbraid.org/datacube> ;
111	      sh:select """SELECT $this
112	WHERE {
113		# Observation in a measureType-cube
114		$this qb:dataSet/qb:structure ?dsd ;
115			qb:measureType ?measure .
116		?dsd qb:component/qb:componentProperty qb:measureType .
117		# Must have value for its measureType
118		FILTER NOT EXISTS { $this ?measure [] }
119	}""" ;
120	    ] ;
121	  sh:sparql [
122	      rdfs:comment "IC-16. Single measure on measure dimension observation" ;
123	      sh:message """In a qb:DataSet which uses a Measure dimension then each qb:Observation must only have a value for one measure (by IC-15 this will be the measure corresponding to its qb:measureType).
124	""" ;
125	      sh:prefixes <http://topbraid.org/datacube> ;
126	      sh:select """SELECT $this
127	WHERE {
128		# Observation with measureType
129		$this qb:dataSet/qb:structure ?dsd ;
130			qb:measureType ?measure ;
131			?omeasure [] .
132		# Any measure on the observation
133		?dsd qb:component/qb:componentProperty qb:measureType ;
134			qb:component/qb:componentProperty ?omeasure .
135		?omeasure a qb:MeasureProperty .
136		# Must be the same as the measureType
137		FILTER (?omeasure != ?measure)
138	}""" ;
139	    ] ;
140	  sh:sparql [
141	      rdfs:comment "IC-17. All measures present in measures dimension cube" ;
142	      sh:message "In a qb:DataSet which uses a Measure dimension then if there is a Observation for some combination of non-measure dimensions then there must be other Observations with the same non-measure dimension values for each of the declared measures." ;
143	      sh:prefixes <http://topbraid.org/datacube> ;
144	      sh:select """SELECT $this
145	WHERE {
146		{
147			# Count number of other measures found at each point
148			SELECT $this ?numMeasures (COUNT(?obs2) AS ?count)
149			WHERE {
150				{
151					# Find the DSDs and check how many measures they have
152					SELECT $this ?dsd (COUNT(?m) AS ?numMeasures)
153					WHERE {
154						?dsd qb:component/qb:componentProperty ?m.
155						?m a qb:MeasureProperty .
156					}
157					GROUP BY ?dsd
158				}
159				# Observation in measureType cube
160				$this qb:dataSet/qb:structure ?dsd;
161					qb:dataSet ?dataset ;
162					qb:measureType ?m1 .
163	
164				# Other observation at same dimension value
165				?obs2 qb:dataSet ?dataset ;
166					qb:measureType ?m2 .
167				FILTER NOT EXISTS {
168					?dsd qb:component/qb:componentProperty ?dim .
169					FILTER (?dim != qb:measureType)
170					?dim a qb:DimensionProperty .
171					$this ?dim ?v1 .
172					?obs2 ?dim ?v2.
173					FILTER (?v1 != ?v2)
174				}
175			}
176			GROUP BY $this ?numMeasures
177			HAVING (?count != ?numMeasures)
178		}
179	}""" ;
180	    ] ;
181	  sh:sparql [
182	      rdfs:comment "IC-18. Consistent data set links" ;
183	      sh:message "If a qb:DataSet D has a qb:slice S, and S has an qb:observation O, then the qb:dataSet corresponding to O must be D." ;
184	      sh:prefixes <http://topbraid.org/datacube> ;
185	      sh:select """SELECT $this
186	WHERE {
187		?slice qb:observation $this .
188		?dataset qb:slice ?slice .
189	    FILTER NOT EXISTS { $this qb:dataSet ?dataset . }
190	}""" ;
191	    ] ;
192	  sh:sparql [
193	      rdfs:comment "IC-19. a) Codes from code list" ;
194	      owl:versionInfo "See section IC-19 in the Data Cubes spec on pre-conditions that need to be met prior to the execution of this constraints. Parts of them are covered by the rules at skos:memberListShape." ;
195	      sh:message "If a dimension property has a qb:codeList, then the value of the dimension property on every qb:Observation must be in the code list." ;
196	      sh:prefixes <http://topbraid.org/datacube> ;
197	      sh:select """SELECT $this
198	WHERE {
199	    $this qb:dataSet/qb:structure/qb:component/qb:componentProperty ?dim .
200	    ?dim a qb:DimensionProperty ;
201	        qb:codeList ?list .
202	    ?list a skos:ConceptScheme .
203	    $this ?dim ?v .
204	    FILTER NOT EXISTS { ?v a skos:Concept ; skos:inScheme ?list }
205	}""" ;
206	    ] ;
207	  sh:sparql [
208	      rdfs:comment "IC-19. b) Codes from code list" ;
209	      owl:versionInfo "See section IC-19 in the Data Cubes spec on pre-conditions that need to be met prior to the execution of this constraints. Parts of them are covered by the rules at skos:memberListShape." ;
210	      sh:message "If a dimension property has a qb:codeList, then the value of the dimension property on every qb:Observation must be in the code list." ;
211	      sh:prefixes <http://topbraid.org/datacube> ;
212	      sh:select """SELECT $this
213	WHERE {
214	    $this qb:dataSet/qb:structure/qb:component/qb:componentProperty ?dim .
215	    ?dim a qb:DimensionProperty ;
216	        qb:codeList ?list .
217	    ?list a skos:Collection .
218	    $this ?dim ?v .
219	    FILTER NOT EXISTS { ?v a skos:Concept ; skos:member+ ?v }
220	}""" ;
221	    ] ;
222	  sh:sparql [
223	      rdfs:comment "IC-20. Codes from hierarchy" ;
224	      sh:message "If a dimension property has a qb:HierarchicalCodeList with a non-blank qb:parentChildProperty then the value of that dimension property on every qb:Observation must be reachable from a root of the hierarchy using zero or more hops along the qb:parentChildProperty links." ;
225	      sh:prefixes <http://topbraid.org/datacube> ;
226	      sh:select """SELECT $this
227	WHERE {
228		$this qb:dataSet/qb:structure/qb:component/qb:componentProperty ?dim .
229		?dim a qb:DimensionProperty ;
230			qb:codeList ?list .
231		?list a qb:HierarchicalCodeList .
232		$this ?dim ?v .
233		?hierarchy a qb:HierarchicalCodeList ;
234			qb:parentChildProperty ?p .
235		FILTER ( isIRI(?p) ) .
236		FILTER NOT EXISTS {
237			?list qb:hierarchyRoot ?root .
238			FILTER qb:hasZeroOrMore(?root, ?p, ?v) .
239		}
240	}""" ;
241	    ] ;
242	  sh:sparql [
243	      rdfs:comment "IC-21. Codes from hierarchy (inverse)" ;
244	      sh:message "If a dimension property has a qb:HierarchicalCodeList with an inverse qb:parentChildProperty then the value of that dimension property on every qb:Observation must be reachable from a root of the hierarchy using zero or more hops along the inverse qb:parentChildProperty links." ;
245	      sh:prefixes <http://topbraid.org/datacube> ;
246	      sh:select """SELECT $this
247	WHERE {
248		$this qb:dataSet/qb:structure/qb:component/qb:componentProperty ?dim .
249		?dim a qb:DimensionProperty ;
250			qb:codeList ?list .
251		?list a qb:HierarchicalCodeList .
252		$this ?dim ?v .
253		?hierarchy a qb:HierarchicalCodeList;
254			qb:parentChildProperty ?pcp .
255		FILTER( isBlank(?pcp) )
256		?pcp  owl:inverseOf ?p .
257		FILTER( isIRI(?p) )
258		FILTER NOT EXISTS {
259			?list qb:hierarchyRoot ?root .
260			FILTER qb:hasZeroOrMore(?root, ?p, ?v) .
261		}
262	}""" ;
263	    ] ;
264	  sh:targetClass qb:Observation ;
265	.

536	def test_sparql_message_subst():
537	    df = '''@prefix ex: <http://datashapes.org/sh/tests/#> .
538	    @prefix owl: <http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#> .
539	    @prefix rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#> .
540	    @prefix rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#> .
541	    @prefix sh: <http://www.w3.org/ns/shacl#> .
542	    @prefix xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#> .
543	
544	    ex:ValidResource1
545	      rdf:type rdfs:Resource ;
546	    .
547	    ex:InvalidResource1
548	      rdf:type rdfs:Resource ;
549	      rdfs:label "Invalid resource 1" ;
550	    .
551	    ex:InvalidResource2
552	      rdf:type rdfs:Resource ;
553	      rdfs:label "Invalid label 1" ;
554	      rdfs:label "Invalid label 2" ;
555	    .
556	    ex:TestShape
557	      rdf:type sh:NodeShape ;
558	      rdfs:label "Test shape" ;
559	      sh:sparql ex:TestShape-sparql ;
560	      sh:targetNode ex:InvalidResource1 ;
561	      sh:targetNode ex:InvalidResource2 ;
562	      sh:targetNode ex:ValidResource1 ;
563	    .
564	    ex:TestShape-sparql
565	      sh:message "{$this} cannot have a {$path} of {$value}" ;
566	      sh:prefixes <http://datashapes.org/sh/tests/sparql/node/sparql-001.test> ;
567	      sh:select """
